    –ú–∞—Ç–µ—Ä—ñ–∞–ª

    JavaScript: –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å, Promise, async/await —Ç–∞ –º–æ–¥—É–ª—ñ

    1. –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    JavaScript ‚Äî –æ–¥–Ω–æ–ø–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∞ –º–æ–≤–∞. –¶–µ –æ–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞—î, —â–æ –≤ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç —á–∞—Å—É –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –ª–∏—à–µ –æ–¥–Ω–∞ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ—è.

    –Ø–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –¥–æ–≤–≥—ñ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ—ó (–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç–∏ –¥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞, —Ç–∞–π–º–µ—Ä–∏, —á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤) —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ ‚Äî —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫–∞ ¬´–∑–∞–≤–º—Ä–µ¬ª.

    –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ç–∞–∫—ñ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ—ó —É —Ñ–æ–Ω—ñ, –Ω–µ –±–ª–æ–∫—É—é—á–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ—Ç—ñ–∫ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è.

    2. –°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∏–π –∫–æ–¥

    –£ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–º—É –∫–æ–¥—ñ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è –π–¥–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ —á–µ—Ä–∑—ñ. –ù–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏–π —Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞—î—Ç—å—Å—è, –ø–æ–∫–∏ –ø–æ–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—ñ–π –Ω–µ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–∏—Ç—å—Å—è. 

    
// —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∞ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è
function calcTax(tax1, tax2) {
  const totalTax = (tax1 + tax2) * 0.85;
  console.log(totalTax);
}

console.log("Start calculation");
calcTax(200, 100);
console.log("End calculation");

    üëâ –ü–æ–∫–∏ calcTax –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è ‚Äî —ñ–Ω—à–∏–π –∫–æ–¥ —á–µ–∫–∞—Ç–∏–º–µ.

    3. –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∏–π –∫–æ–¥ —Ç–∞ setTimeout

    setTimeout –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –≤—ñ–¥–∫–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó —ñ –Ω–µ –±–ª–æ–∫—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ—Ç—ñ–∫. 

    
function calcTax(tax1, tax2) {
  const totalTax = (tax1 + tax2) * 0.85;

  setTimeout(function () {
    console.log(totalTax);
  }, 2500);
}

console.log("Start calculation");
calcTax(200, 100);
console.log("End calculation");

    üëâ –°–ø–æ—á–∞—Ç–∫—É –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–µ—Ç—å—Å—è Start —ñ End, —ñ –ª–∏—à–µ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ 2.5 —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥–∏ ‚Äî —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç.

    4. Callback-—Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó

    Callback ‚Äî —Ü–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è, —è–∫—É –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—é—Ç—å —è–∫ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç —ñ –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫–∞—é—Ç—å –ø—ñ–∑–Ω—ñ—à–µ. 

    
console.log("Request to server...");

setTimeout(function fetchData() {
  console.log("Loading...");

  const serverData = {
    user: "Employee10",
    id: 122,
    location: "Lviv"
  };

  setTimeout(function showData() {
    serverData.received = true;
    console.log("Data loaded:", serverData);
  }, 1500);

}, 1500);

console.log("Other activities");

    üëâ –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω—ñ callback-–∏ –ø–æ—Ç—Ä–∞–ø–ª—è—é—Ç—å —É —á–µ—Ä–≥—É —ñ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—é—Ç—å—Å—è –ø—ñ—Å–ª—è —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–¥—É.

    5. –ù–µ–¥–æ–ª—ñ–∫–∏ callback

    • callback hell (–≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–µ–Ω—ñ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó)
    • —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω–∞ –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–∫–∞ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–æ–∫
    • –Ω–µ–º–æ–∂–ª–∏–≤–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ return

    üëâ –°–∞–º–µ —Ç–æ–º—É –∑ º—è–≤–∏–ª–∏—Å—è Promise.

    6. Promise: —â–æ —Ü–µ —Ç–∞–∫–µ

    Promise ‚Äî —Ü–µ –æ–± º—î–∫—Ç, —è–∫–∏–π –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—î —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ—ó –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –≤ –º–∞–π–±—É—Ç–Ω—å–æ–º—É.

    –°—Ç–∞–Ω Promise:

    • pending ‚Äî –æ—á—ñ–∫—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è
    • fulfilled ‚Äî —É—Å–ø—ñ—Ö
    • rejected ‚Äî –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∞

    7. –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è Promise

    
const willIGetPremium = new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
  const isBossHappy = true;

  if (isBossHappy) {
    resolve({ kind: "premium", amount: 500 });
  } else {
    reject(new Error("Premium rejected"));
  }
});

    üëâ resolve ‚Äî —É—Å–ø—ñ—Ö, reject ‚Äî –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∞.

    8. then —Ç–∞ catch

    
willIGetPremium
  .then(function (result) {
    console.log(result);
  })
  .catch(function (error) {
    console.log(error.message);
  });

    üëâ then ‚Äî –¥–ª—è —É—Å–ø—ñ—Ö—É, catch ‚Äî –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∏.

    9. –õ–∞–Ω—Ü—é–∂–∫–∏ Promise

    
new Promise(resolve => {
  setTimeout(() => resolve(1), 2000);
})
.then(result => {
  console.log(result);
  return result * 2;
})
.then(result => {
  console.log(result);
  return result * 2;
});

    üëâ –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è, —è–∫–µ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î then, –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—î—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–∞–ª—ñ –ø–æ –ª–∞–Ω—Ü—é–∂–∫—É.

    10. async / await

    async / await ‚Äî —Ü–µ —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—Å –Ω–∞–¥ Promise, —è–∫–∏–π —Ä–æ–±–∏—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥ —á–∏—Ç–∞–±–µ–ª—å–Ω–∏–º. 

    
async function loadData() {
  const result = await new Promise(resolve => {
    setTimeout(() => resolve("Done"), 2000);
  });

  console.log(result);
}

loadData();

    üëâ await –∑—É–ø–∏–Ω—è—î –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó, –∞–ª–µ –Ω–µ –±–ª–æ–∫—É—î –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä.

    11. –û–±—Ä–æ–±–∫–∞ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–æ–∫ –≤ async/await

    
async function getData() {
  try {
    const response = await fetch("https://no-such-url");
  } catch (error) {
    console.log(error);
  }

    üëâ –í–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –∑–≤–∏—á–∞–π–Ω–∏–π try / catch.

    12. –ú–æ–¥—É–ª—ñ –≤ JavaScript

    –ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å ‚Äî —Ü–µ –æ–∫—Ä–µ–º–∏–π JS-—Ñ–∞–π–ª, —è–∫–∏–π –µ–∫—Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—É—î —Ç–∞ —ñ–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—É—î –∫–æ–¥.

    –ü–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∞–≥–∏:

    • —ñ–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü—ñ—è –∫–æ–¥—É
    • –ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω–µ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è
    • –≤—ñ–¥—Å—É—Ç–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å –≥–ª–æ–±–∞–ª—å–Ω–∏—Ö –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ö

    13. export —Ç–∞ import

  return a + b;
}

    14. export default

    this.name = name;
  }

    üëâ export default –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ —Ç—ñ–ª—å–∫–∏ –æ–¥–∏–Ω —É —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ.

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    –ü—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è: Asynchronous JavaScript, Promise, async/await, Modules

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 1. setTimeout —ñ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    –Ñ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–∞ "–ü–æ—á–∞—Ç–∏" —Ç–∞ –ø–æ—Ä–æ–∂–Ω—ñ–π –±–ª–æ–∫.

    • –ø—Ä–∏ –∫–ª—ñ–∫—É –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å "Start"
    • —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ setTimeout —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ 2 —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥–∏ –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ "Async task"
    • –æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑—É –ø—ñ—Å–ª—è –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫—É setTimeout –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ "End"
    • –ø–æ—è—Å–Ω–∏ (–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ä–µ–º), —á–æ–º—É "End" –∑ º—è–≤–ª—è—î—Ç—å—Å—è —Ä–∞–Ω—ñ—à–µ

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 2. Callback-—Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é loadData(callback), —è–∫–∞ —ñ–º—ñ—Ç—É—î –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –¥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞.

    • –≤—Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∏–Ω—ñ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–π setTimeout (2 —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥–∏)
    • –ø—ñ—Å–ª—è –∑–∞—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∫–∏ —Å—Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É–π –æ–± º—î–∫—Ç –∑ –¥–∞–Ω–∏–º–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞
    • –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–π —Ü—ñ –¥–∞–Ω—ñ —É callback-—Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é
    • –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–π callback –¥–ª—è –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö —É DOM

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 3. Callback hell

    –ó—ñ–º—ñ—Ç—É–π –ø–æ—Å–ª—ñ–¥–æ–≤–Ω–µ –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö.

    • –ø–µ—Ä—à–∏–π setTimeout ‚Äî "–ó–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞"
    • –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–π –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–π setTimeout ‚Äî "–ó–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–æ–≤–∞—Ä—ñ–≤"
    • —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—ñ–π –≤–∫–ª–∞–¥–µ–Ω–∏–π setTimeout ‚Äî "–ó–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –∑–∞–º–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω—å"

    console.log("Async task");
    document.querySelector("#set-text").textContent = `"Async task"`;

  console.log("End");
  document.querySelector("#end-text").textContent = `"End"`;
});

const userInfo = document.querySelector("#user-info");

function loadData(callback) {
  setTimeout(() => {
    const user = {
      name: "Igor",
      age: 21,
      city: "Kyiv",
    };

    callback(user);
  }, 2000);
}

function renderUser(userData) {
  userInfo.textContent = `Name: ${userData.name}, Age: ${userData.age}, City: ${userData.city}`;
}

loadData(renderUser);

//  Task 4

const userName = document.querySelector("#user-name");
const userAge = document.querySelector("#user-age");
const userRole = document.querySelector("#user-role");
const checkUserBtn = document.querySelector("#check-user");
const usersInfo = document.querySelector("#users-info");

function setUserRole(user) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => {
      const age = Number(user.age);
      const name = user.name;

      if (!age || !name) {
        reject(new Error(`empty input`));
      } else if (age >= 18) {
        user.role = "admin";
        user.isAccess = true;
        resolve(`${name} get "${user.role}" role`);
      } else {
        user.role = "user";
        user.isAccess = false;
        reject(new Error(`${name} too young`));
      }
    }, 1500);
  });
}

checkUserBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  const user = {
    name: userName.value,
    age: userAge.value,
    role: userRole.value,
    isAccess: false,
  };

  usersInfo.textContent = "Checking...";

  setUserRole(user)
    .then((data) => {
      usersInfo.textContent = data;
      userRole.value = user.role;
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      usersInfo.textContent = error.message;
      userRole.value = user.role || "undefined";
    });
});

//  Task 5

const inputNum = document.querySelector("#input-num");
const outputFirst = document.querySelector("#output-first");
const outputSecond = document.querySelector("#output-second");
const outputThird = document.querySelector("#output-third");

function numPromise(num) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const parsedNum = Number(num);

    resolve(parsedNum);
  });
}

inputNum.addEventListener("input", () => {
  const num = inputNum.value;

  numPromise(num)
    .then((result) => {
      outputFirst.textContent = `Initial: ${result}`;
      return result * 2;
    })
    .then((result) => {
      outputSecond.textContent = `Multiplied by 2: ${result}`;
      return result + 10;
    })
    .then((result) => {
      outputThird.textContent = `Added 10: ${result}`;
    });
});

// Task 6

const outputAllPromises = document.querySelector("#output-all-promises");

const userData = new Promise((resolve) => {
  setTimeout(() => {
    resolve({ name: "bob", age: 22, role: "customer" });
  }, 2000);
});

const goodsData = new Promise((resolve) => {
  setTimeout(() => {
    resolve([
      { name: "sugar", quantity: 10 },
      { name: "salt", quantity: 20 },
    ]);
  }, 500);
});

Promise.all([userData, goodsData])
  .then(([user, goods]) => {
    const userHTML = `
      
    
        
    User: ${user.name}
    
        
    Role: ${user.role}, Age: ${user.age}
    
      
    
    `;

    const goodsHTML = `
      
      
        ${goods.map((item) => `
    • ${item.name} ‚Äî ${item.quantity}
      • `).join("")}
      
    
    `;

    outputAllPromises.innerHTML = `${userHTML} 
    Goods:
     ${goodsHTML}`;
  })
  .catch((err) => {
    outputAllPromises.textContent = "Error: " + err.message;
  });

// Task 7

const outputAwait = document.querySelector("#output-await");
const outputPromise = document.querySelector("#output-promise");

function testPromis() {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => resolve("Stop-stop-stop"), 1000);
  });
}

testPromis().then((result) => {
  outputPromise.textContent = result;
  console.log(result);
});

async function testAwait() {
  const promise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => resolve("Go-go-go"), 1500);
  });
  const result = await promise;
  outputAwait.textContent = result;
  console.log(result);
}
testAwait();

// Task 8

const outputError = document.querySelector("#output-error");

async function func() {
  const promis = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Some error")), 1500);
  });
  try {
    const result = await promis;
    console.log(result);
  } catch (error) {
    outputError.textContent = error.message;
  }
}
func();

import { getUser } from "./script2.js";

const outputModule = document.querySelector("#output-module");

async function render() {
  outputModule.textContent = "Loading...";
  try {
    const user = await getUser();

    outputModule.textContent = `User: ${user.name}, Age: ${user.age}, Role: ${user.role}`;
  } catch (error) {
    outputModule.textContent = "Error loading user";
  }
}

render();

// Task 10

const addNewUserBtn = document.querySelector("#add-new-user");
const newUserName = document.querySelector("#new-user-name");
const outputList = document.querySelector("#users-list");

const usersMap = new Map();

async function saveUser(id, name) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (!name) {
        reject(new Error("Fields cannot be empty!"));
      } else {
        resolve({ id, name });
      }
    }, 1000);
  });
}

async function addNewUser() {
  const name = newUserName.value.trim();
  const id = Date.now();

  try {
    outputList.innerHTML += `
  • Saving ${name}...
    • `;

    const savedUser = await saveUser(id, name);

    usersMap.set(savedUser.id, savedUser.name);
  } catch (error) {
    alert("Error: " + error.message);
  }
  renderUsers();
}

function renderUsers() {
  outputList.innerHTML = "";
  usersMap.forEach((id, name) => {
    outputList.innerHTML += `
  • ${name} has ${id}
    • `;
  });
}

addNewUserBtn.addEventListener("click", addNewUser);

    1. –©–æ —Ç–∞–∫–µ Node.js

    Node.js ‚Äî —Ü–µ JavaScript runtime, —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π —É 2009 —Ä–æ—Ü—ñ.

    –¶–µ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≤–∞ —ñ –Ω–µ —Ñ—Ä–µ–π–º–≤–æ—Ä–∫, –∞ —Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤–∏—â–µ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è JavaScript –ø–æ–∑–∞ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–æ–º.

    • –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –Ω–∞ —Ä—É—à—ñ—ó V8 (—è–∫ —É Google Chrome)
    • –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–∏–π –Ω–∞ C++ —Ç–∞ JavaScript
    • –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –Ω–∞ Windows, Linux, macOS

    2. –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ñ –æ—Å–æ–±–ª–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—ñ Node.js

    • –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∏–π —Ç–∞ –ø–æ–¥—ñ—î–≤–∏–π ‚Äî –Ω–µ–±–ª–æ–∫—É—é—á—ñ API
    • –®–≤–∏–¥–∫–∏–π ‚Äî –∑–∞–≤–¥—è–∫–∏ V8
    • –û–¥–Ω–æ–ø–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π, –∞–ª–µ –¥–æ–±—Ä–µ –º–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è
    • –ë–µ–∑ –±—É—Ñ–µ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—ó ‚Äî –¥–∞–Ω—ñ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—é—Ç—å—Å—è —á–∞–Ω–∫–∞–º–∏

    3. –ê—Ä—Ö—ñ—Ç–µ–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ Node.js

    Node.js —ñ–¥–µ–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø—ñ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –¥–ª—è I/O-—ñ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Å–∏–≤–Ω–∏—Ö –∑–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Å—É–Ω–∫—ñ–≤.

    –í –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ñ –ª–µ–∂–∏—Ç—å event loop, —è–∫–∏–π –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–ª—è—Ç–∏ —Ç–∏—Å—è—á—ñ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—ñ–≤ –±–µ–∑ —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ö –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫—ñ–≤.

    4. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∞–≥–∏ —Ç–∞ –Ω–µ–¥–æ–ª—ñ–∫–∏

    –ü–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∞–≥–∏

    • —à–≤–∏–¥–∫–∏–π
    • –º–∞—Å—à—Ç–∞–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π
    • –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–∞ –µ–∫–æ—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞

    –ù–µ–¥–æ–ª—ñ–∫–∏

    • –Ω–µ –ø—ñ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –¥–ª—è CPU-–≤–∞–∂–∫–∏—Ö –∑–∞–¥–∞—á
    • —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω–∞ –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª—å –¥–ª—è –Ω–æ–≤–∞—á–∫—ñ–≤
    • API –º–æ–∂–µ –∑–º—ñ–Ω—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è

    • Front-end —ñ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏ (Webpack, Vite)

    7. –ü–æ–ø—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω—ñ –º–æ–¥—É–ª—ñ

    9. package.json

    –§–∞–π–ª package.json –º—ñ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—é –ø—Ä–æ –ø—Ä–æ—î–∫—Ç —Ç–∞ –∑–∞–ª–µ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—ñ.

  "name": "node-sample",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "dependencies": {
    "express": "^4.18.0"
  }
}

// Task 1

// Node.js ‚Äî —Ü–µ —Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤–∏—â–µ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è, —è–∫–µ –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ JavaScript-–∫–æ–¥ –ø–æ–∑–∞ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–æ–º
// (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥, –Ω–∞ —Ç–≤–æ—î–º—É –∫–æ–º–ø'—é—Ç–µ—Ä—ñ –∞–±–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä—ñ). –ë–µ–∑ –Ω—å–æ–≥–æ JS –±—É–≤ –±–∏ –æ–±–º–µ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π –ª–∏—à–µ –≤–µ–±—Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫–∞–º–∏.

// NPM (Node Package Manager) ‚Äî —Ü–µ –≥—ñ–≥–∞–Ω—Ç—Å—å–∫–∞ "–±—ñ–±–ª—ñ–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∞" —Ç–∞ –º–µ–Ω–µ–¥–∂–µ—Ä –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç—ñ–≤. –í—ñ–Ω –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º—ñ—Å—Ç–∞–º
// –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ñ —ñ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏, –º–æ–¥—É–ª—ñ —Ç–∞ —Ñ—Ä–µ–π–º–≤–æ—Ä–∫–∏ (—è–∫-–æ—Ç React –∞–±–æ Express), —â–æ–± –Ω–µ –ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç–∏ –≤—Å–µ –∑ –Ω—É–ª—è.

// –û—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∞ —Ä—ñ–∑–Ω–∏—Ü—è –ø–æ–ª—è–≥–∞—î –≤ —Ç–æ–º—É, —â–æ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –∑ —ñ–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–æ–º –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞ —Ç–∞ DOM, —Ç–æ–¥—ñ —è–∫ Node.js –º–∞—î –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø

// Task 4 & 5
const http = require("http");

http
  .createServer((request, response) => {
    // response.writeHead(200, { "Content-Type": "text/plain" });
    // response.write("Node.js server works");
    console.log(`–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É: ${request.method}`);
    console.log(`–ó–∞–ø–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–∏–π URL: ${request.url}`);
    response.writeHead(200, { "Content-Type": "text/html; charset=utf-8" });
    response.write("
    Node.js server works
    ");
    response.write(
      `
    –í–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥: ${request.method} –¥–ª—è —à–ª—è—Ö—É: ${request.url}
    `,
    );
    response.end();
  })
  .listen(3000);
console.log("Server running at http://127.0.0.1:3000/");

// request (req): –¶–µ –æ–±'—î–∫—Ç-–ø–æ—Ç—ñ–∫, —è–∫–∏–π –º—ñ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å —É—Å—é —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—é –ø—Ä–æ –≤—Ö—ñ–¥–Ω–∏–π –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –≤—ñ–¥ –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç–∞ (–±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞).
//  –ß–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –Ω—å–æ–≥–æ –º–∏ –¥—ñ–∑–Ω–∞—î–º–æ—Å—è, —è–∫—É —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫—É —Ö–æ—á–µ –≤—ñ–¥–∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á (url), —è–∫–∏–π –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î
// (GET, POST), —è–∫—ñ –¥–∞–Ω—ñ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—î —Ç–∞ —è–∫—ñ –≤ –Ω—å–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–∫–∏ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥, —Ç–∏–ø –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞).

// response (res): –¶–µ –æ–±'—î–∫—Ç-–ø–æ—Ç—ñ–∫, —è–∫–∏–π –º–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î–º–æ –¥–ª—è —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—ñ. –ó–∞ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–æ—é
// –Ω—å–æ–≥–æ –º–∏ –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª—é—î–º–æ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å-–∫–æ–¥ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥, 200 OK –∞–±–æ 404 Not Found), —Ç–∏–ø–∏ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç—É —Ç–∞, –≤–ª–∞—Å–Ω–µ,
// –≤—ñ–¥–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—î–º–æ –¥–∞–Ω—ñ (—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç, HTML –∞–±–æ JSON) –Ω–∞–∑–∞–¥ —É –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä.
    –ú–∞—Ç–µ—Ä—ñ–∞–ª

    –í–∑–∞—î–º–æ–¥—ñ—è –∑ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–º: HTTP, AJAX —Ç–∞ Fetch API

    1. –í–∑–∞—î–º–æ–¥—ñ—è –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞ –∑ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–º

    –ë—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∏–π –≤–µ–±–∑–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Å—É–Ω–æ–∫ –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –∑–∞ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–ª—é –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç ‚Äì —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä. –ë—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä (–∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç) –Ω–∞–¥—Å–∏–ª–∞—î –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç, —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–ª—è—î –π–æ–≥–æ —Ç–∞ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—å.

    –î–ª—è —Ü—ñ—î—ó –≤–∑–∞—î–º–æ–¥—ñ—ó –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª HTTP.

    2. HTTP ‚Äî —â–æ —Ü–µ —Ç–∞–∫–µ

    HTTP (HyperText Transfer Protocol) ‚Äî —Ü–µ –ø—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω–∏–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª –¥–ª—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –≥—ñ–ø–µ—Ä—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç–æ–≤–∏—Ö –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ (HTML) –º—ñ–∂ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–æ–º —ñ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–º.

    • –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é—î –∑–∞ –º–æ–¥–µ–ª–ª—é –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç‚Äì—Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä
    • —î stateless (—Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –Ω–µ –∑–±–µ—Ä—ñ–≥–∞—î —Å—Ç–∞–Ω –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç–∞)
    • –∫–æ–∂–µ–Ω –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–ª—è—î—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–µ–∑–∞–ª–µ–∂–Ω–æ

    3. –°—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ HTTP-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É

    HTTP-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–∞—î—Ç—å—Å—è –∑:

    • –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—É (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE —Ç–æ—â–æ)
    • URL (–∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å–∏ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å—É)
    • –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–∫—ñ–≤ (headers)
    • —Ç—ñ–ª–∞ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É (body, –Ω–µ –∑–∞–≤–∂–¥–∏)

    4. –°—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ HTTP-–≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—ñ

    HTTP-–≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—å –º—ñ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å:

    • –∫–æ–¥ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å—É (200, 404, 500‚Ä¶)
    • –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–∫–∏
    • —Ç—ñ–ª–æ –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—ñ (HTML, JSON, —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç)

    5. HTTP-–º–µ—Ç–æ–¥–∏

    • GET ‚Äî –æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∞–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö
    • POST ‚Äî –Ω–∞–¥—Å–∏–ª–∞–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö
    • PUT ‚Äî –ø–æ–≤–Ω–µ –æ–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å—É
    • PATCH ‚Äî —á–∞—Å—Ç–∫–æ–≤–µ –æ–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è
    • DELETE ‚Äî –≤–∏–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è
    • OPTIONS ‚Äî —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—è –ø—Ä–æ –º–æ–∂–ª–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—ñ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞

    6. HTTP —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—É—Å-–∫–æ–¥–∏

    • 1xx ‚Äî —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ–π–Ω—ñ
    • 2xx ‚Äî —É—Å–ø—ñ—à–Ω—ñ
    • 3xx ‚Äî –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è
    • 4xx ‚Äî –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∏ –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç–∞
    • 5xx ‚Äî –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∏ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞

    7. –Ü–¥–µ–º–ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å HTTP-–º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ñ–≤

    –Ü–¥–µ–º–ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–∏–π –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥ ‚Äî —Ü–µ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥, –ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω–∏–π –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫ —è–∫–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –∑–º—ñ–Ω—é—î —Å—Ç–∞–Ω —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞.

    –Ü–¥–µ–º–ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω—ñ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥–∏:

    • GET
    • PUT
    • DELETE
    • HEAD

    –ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥ POST ‚Äî –Ω–µ —ñ–¥–µ–º–ø–æ—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω–∏–π.

    8. Stateless –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª

    HTTP ‚Äî stateless, —Ç–æ–±—Ç–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –Ω–µ –ø–∞–º º—è—Ç–∞—î –ø–æ–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç–∏ –∫–ª—ñ—î–Ω—Ç–∞.

    –ö–æ–∂–µ–Ω –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –º–∞—î –º—ñ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–∏ –≤—Å—é –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö—ñ–¥–Ω—É —ñ–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü—ñ—é –¥–ª—è –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–∫–∏.

    9. AJAX

    AJAX (Asynchronous JavaScript and XML) ‚Äî —Ü–µ –ø—ñ–¥—Ö—ñ–¥, —è–∫–∏–π –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω—ñ –∑ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –±–µ–∑ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫–∏.

    –ü–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∞–≥–∏ AJAX:

    • —à–≤–∏–¥—à–∞ –≤–∑–∞—î–º–æ–¥—ñ—è
    • –æ–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫–∏
    • –∫—Ä–∞—â–∏–π UX

    10. –¢–µ—Ö–Ω–æ–ª–æ–≥—ñ—ó AJAX

    • JavaScript ‚Äî –ª–æ–≥—ñ–∫–∞
    • DOM ‚Äî –æ–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫–∏
    • CSS ‚Äî —Å—Ç–∏–ª—ñ
    • XMLHttpRequest ‚Äî –æ–±–º—ñ–Ω –∑ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–º

    11. XMLHttpRequest

    
const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();

xhr.open("GET", "data.json", true);

xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
  if (xhr.readyState === 4 && xhr.status === 200) {
    console.log(xhr.responseText);
  }
};

xhr.send();

    12. ReadyState

    • 0 ‚Äî UNSENT
    • 1 ‚Äî OPENED
    • 2 ‚Äî HEADERS_RECEIVED
    • 3 ‚Äî LOADING
    • 4 ‚Äî DONE

    13. Fetch API

    Fetch API ‚Äî —Å—É—á–∞—Å–Ω–∞ –∞–ª—å—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤–∞ XMLHttpRequest, –ø–æ–±—É–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ Promise. 

    
fetch("https://api.github.com/users/octocat")
  .then(response => response.json())
  .then(data => console.log(data));

    14. Fetch API –∑ async / await

    
async function loadUser() {
  const response = await fetch("https://api.github.com/users/octocat");
  const data = await response.json();
  console.log(data);
}

loadUser();

    15. POST-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Fetch

    
fetch("https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts", {
  method: "POST",
  headers: {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
  },
  body: JSON.stringify({
    title: "Post title",
    body: "Post content",
    userId: 1
  })
})
.then(response => response.json())
.then(data => console.log(data));

    16. Same Origin Policy

    –ë—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∏ –æ–±–º–µ–∂—É—é—Ç—å AJAX-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç–∏ –º—ñ–∂ —Ä—ñ–∑–Ω–∏–º–∏ –¥–æ–º–µ–Ω–∞–º–∏ –∑ –º—ñ—Ä–∫—É–≤–∞–Ω—å –±–µ–∑–ø–µ–∫–∏.

    –î–ª—è –æ–±—Ö–æ–¥—É –æ–±–º–µ–∂–µ–Ω—å –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é—Ç—å CORS –∞–±–æ JSONP.

    17. –ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å–Ω—ñ –ø–æ—Å–∏–ª–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    • javascript.info ‚Äî fetch

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    –ü—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è: AJAX —Ç–∞ Fetch API

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 1. –ü–µ—Ä—à–∏–π Fetch-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ HTML-—Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫—É –∑ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫–æ—é Load Users.

    –ü—Ä–∏ –∫–ª—ñ–∫—É –Ω–∞ –∫–Ω–æ–ø–∫—É –ø–æ—Ç—Ä—ñ–±–Ω–æ:

    • –∑—Ä–æ–±–∏—Ç–∏ GET-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –∑–∞ –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å–æ—é https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users
    • –æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∞—Ç–∏ –º–∞—Å–∏–≤ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á—ñ–≤
    • –≤–∏–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á—ñ–≤ —É –≤–∏–≥–ª—è–¥—ñ —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫—É (<ul>)

    –í–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É–π Fetch API.

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 2. Fetch + –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–∫–∞ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–æ–∫

    –ù–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ñ –ø–æ–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—å–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è:

    • –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤—ñ—Ä—è–π response.ok
    • —è–∫—â–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É–≤ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫—É ‚Äî –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ –ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥–æ–º–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è "–ü–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∞ –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö"
    • —É —Ä–∞–∑—ñ —É—Å–ø—ñ—Ö—É ‚Äî –ø–æ–∫–∞–∂–∏ –¥–∞–Ω—ñ

    –í–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É–π .catch() –¥–ª—è –æ–±—Ä–æ–±–∫–∏ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–æ–∫.

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 3. POST-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ Fetch

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É –∑ –ø–æ–ª—è–º–∏:

    • name
    • email

    –ü—Ä–∏ –≤—ñ–¥–ø—Ä–∞–≤—Ü—ñ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏:

    • –≤—ñ–¥–º—ñ–Ω–∏ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—É –ø–æ–≤–µ–¥—ñ–Ω–∫—É —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏
    • –∑—Ä–æ–±–∏ POST-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts
    • –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–π –¥–∞–Ω—ñ —É —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç—ñ JSON
    • –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ –≤—ñ–¥–ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥—å —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ–Ω–∫—É

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 4. XMLHttpRequest (–∫–ª–∞—Å–∏—á–Ω–∏–π AJAX)

    –†–µ–∞–ª—ñ–∑—É–π GET-–∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç –∑–∞ –¥–æ–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–æ—é XMLHttpRequest:

    • URL: https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts
    • –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ –ø–µ—Ä—à—ñ 5 –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–∫—ñ–≤ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—ñ–≤

    –ü–æ—Ä—ñ–≤–Ω—è–π —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—Å —ñ–∑ Fetch API.

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 5. Fetch + async / await

    –ü–µ—Ä–µ–ø–∏—à–∏ –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–µ –ø–æ–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–Ω—î –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è, –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é—á–∏:

    • async / await
    • try / catch

    –ó–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–∏ —É–≤–∞–≥—É –Ω–∞ —á–∏—Ç–∞–±–µ–ª—å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥—É.

    –î–æ–¥–∞—Ç–∫–æ–≤–æ (–Ω–µ–æ–±–æ–≤ º—è–∑–∫–æ–≤–æ)

    –î–æ–¥–∞–π —ñ–Ω–¥–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è (Loading...) –ø—ñ–¥ —á–∞—Å –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è –∑–∞–ø–∏—Ç—É.

// Task 1 & 2 & 5

const loadUsersBtn = document.querySelector("#load-users-btn");
const usersList = document.querySelector("#users-list");

async function getUserName() {
  const url = "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users";
  try {
    const response = await fetch(url);

    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`–ü–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∞ –∑–∞–≤–∞–Ω—Ç–∞–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö`);
    }
    const data = await response.json();
    const htmlContent = data
      .map((user, index) => `
  • ${index + 1}. ${user.name}
    • `)
      .join("");

    usersList.innerHTML = htmlContent;
  } catch (error) {
    usersList.innerHTML = `
  • ${error.message}
    • `;
  }
  loadUsersBtn.disabled = false;
}

loadUsersBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  loadUsersBtn.disabled = true;
  usersList.innerHTML = "Loading...";
  setTimeout(() => {
    getUserName();
  }, 500);
});

// Task 3

const form = document.querySelector("#my-form");
const userName = document.querySelector("#input-name");
const userNameMsg = document.querySelector("#output-name");
const userEmail = document.querySelector("#input-email");
const userEmailMsg = document.querySelector("#output-email");
const outputMsg = document.querySelector("#output-msg");

form.addEventListener("submit", (event) => {
  event.preventDefault();
  let valid = true;

  const newUser = {
    id: Date.now(),
    title: userName.value,
    email: userEmail.value,
  };

  const regMail = /^\w+@[a-z]+\.[a-z]+$/i;
  const emailValue = userEmail.value;

  if (!emailValue) {
    userEmailMsg.textContent = "Error input-field is empty";
    userEmailMsg.classList.add("alert");
    valid = false;
  } else if (regMail.test(emailValue) === false) {
    userEmailMsg.textContent = "Error incorect email";
    userEmailMsg.classList.add("alert");
    valid = false;
  } else {
    userEmailMsg.textContent = "Success your email acepted";
    userEmailMsg.classList.remove("alert");
    userEmailMsg.classList.add("success");
  }

  const regName = /^[a-z]\w{2,15}$/i;
  const nameValue = userName.value;

  if (!nameValue) {
    userNameMsg.textContent = "Error input-field is empty";
    userNameMsg.classList.add("alert");
    valid = false;
  } else if (regName.test(nameValue) === false) {
    userNameMsg.textContent = "Error incorect name";
    userNameMsg.classList.add("alert");
    valid = false;
  } else {
    userNameMsg.textContent = "Success your name acepted";
    userNameMsg.classList.remove("alert");
    userNameMsg.classList.add("success");
  }

  outputMsg.textContent = "Sending error";
  outputMsg.classList.add("alert");

  if (valid) {
    outputMsg.textContent = "Sending...";
    outputMsg.classList.remove("alert");
    outputMsg.classList.add("success");
    fetch("https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify(newUser),
      headers: {
        "Content-type": "application/json; charset=UTF-8",
      },
    })
      .then((response) => {
        if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Server error");
        return response.json();
      })
      .then((json) => {
        outputMsg.textContent = `Success! Server returned ID: ${json.id} user: ${json.title}, email: ${json.email}`;
      })
      .catch((error) => {
        outputMsg.textContent = "Error: " + error.message;
      });

    setTimeout(() => {
      form.reset();
      outputMsg.textContent = "...";
      outputMsg.classList.remove("success");
      userNameMsg.textContent = "...";
      userNameMsg.classList.remove("success");
      userEmailMsg.textContent = "...";
      userEmailMsg.classList.remove("success");
    }, 1000);
  }
});

// Task 4

const loadPostsBtn = document.querySelector("#load-posts-btn");
const postsList = document.querySelector("#posts-list");

function downloadPosts() {
  const ajaxRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
  ajaxRequest.open("GET", "https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/posts", true);
  ajaxRequest.onreadystatechange = function () {
    if (ajaxRequest.readyState != 4) return;
    if (ajaxRequest.status != 200) {
      postsList.textContent = `Error ${ajaxRequest.status}:  ${ajaxRequest.statusText}`;
    } else {
      const postsData = JSON.parse(ajaxRequest.responseText);
      const htmlContent = postsData
        .slice(0, 5)
        .map((post, index) => `
  • ${index + 1}. ${post.title}
    • `)
        .join("");
      loadPostsBtn.disabled = false;
      postsList.innerHTML = htmlContent;
    }
  };
  ajaxRequest.send();
}

loadPostsBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
  loadPostsBtn.disabled = true;
  postsList.innerHTML = "Loading...";
  setTimeout(() => {
    downloadPosts();
  }, 500);
});
    –ú–∞—Ç–µ—Ä—ñ–∞–ª

    TypeScript: –≤—Å—Ç—É–ø, –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ñ —Ç–∏–ø–∏ —Ç–∞ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—è

    1. –©–æ —Ç–∞–∫–µ TypeScript

    TypeScript ‚Äî —Ü–µ –Ω–∞–¥–º–Ω–æ–∂–∏–Ω–∞ JavaScript, —è–∫–∞ –¥–æ–¥–∞—î —Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—á–Ω—É —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—é.

    JavaScript —î –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º—ñ—á–Ω–æ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ—é –º–æ–≤–æ—é, —Ç–æ–º—É —Ç–∏–ø–∏ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∏—Ö –º–æ–∂—É—Ç—å –∑–º—ñ–Ω—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è –ø—ñ–¥ —á–∞—Å –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–∏.

    TypeScript –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –∑–Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç–∏ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∏ –Ω–∞ –µ—Ç–∞–ø—ñ –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–Ω—è –∫–æ–¥—É, –∞ –Ω–µ –ø—ñ–¥ —á–∞—Å –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è.

    2. –¢–∏–ø–æ–≤—ñ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∏ JavaScript

    –£ JavaScript —Ç–∏–ø –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–æ—ó –º–æ–∂–µ –∑–º—ñ–Ω—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏—Å—è –±–µ–∑ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∏:

    let id = 1;     // number

    üëâ –¢–∞–∫—ñ —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü—ñ—ó —É –≤–µ–ª–∏–∫–∏—Ö –ø—Ä–æ—î–∫—Ç–∞—Ö –ø—Ä–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥—è—Ç—å –¥–æ –Ω–µ–æ—á—ñ–∫—É–≤–∞–Ω–∏—Ö –±–∞–≥—ñ–≤.

    3. –Ø–∫ TypeScript –≤–∏—Ä—ñ—à—É—î —Ü—ñ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∏

    • –≤–∏—è–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–æ–∫ –¥–æ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫—É –∫–æ–¥—É
    • –ø–æ–∫—Ä–∞—â–µ–Ω—ñ –ø—ñ–¥–∫–∞–∑–∫–∏ –≤ —Ä–µ–¥–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä—ñ

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    –ü—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è: TypeScript ‚Äî –≤—Å—Ç—É–ø —Ç–∞ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ñ —Ç–∏–ø–∏

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 1. –û–≥–æ–ª–æ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤

    –û–≥–æ–ª–æ—Å–∏ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑ —è–≤–Ω–∏–º –∑–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è–º —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤.

    • –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ userName —Ç–∏–ø—É string
    • –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ age —Ç–∏–ø—É number
    • –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ isAdmin —Ç–∏–ø—É boolean
    • –ø—Ä–∏—Å–≤–æ–π –∫–æ—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—ñ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 2. –ü–æ–º–∏–ª–∫–∞ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—É –∑ —Ç–∏–ø–æ–º number.

    • –ø—Ä–∏—Å–≤–æ–π —ó–π —á–∏—Å–ª–æ
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –ø—Ä–∏—Å–≤–æ—ó—Ç–∏ —Ä—è–¥–æ–∫
    • –ø–æ–¥–∏–≤–∏—Å—å, —è–∫—É –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫—É –ø–æ–∫–∞–∂–µ TypeScript

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 3. –¢–∏–ø any

    –ü—Ä–æ–¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–π —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç—É —Ç–∏–ø—É any.

    • —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—É –∑ —Ç–∏–ø–æ–º any
    • –ø—Ä–∏—Å–≤–æ–π —á–∏—Å–ª–æ, —Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ —ñ boolean
    • –∑—Ä–æ–±–∏ –≤–∏—Å–Ω–æ–≤–æ–∫, —á–æ–º—É —Ü–µ–π —Ç–∏–ø –Ω–µ–±–∞–∂–∞–Ω–∏–π

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 4. –¢–∏–ø—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—è –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é sum.

    • –¥–≤–∞ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∏ —Ç–∏–ø—É number
    • —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î —ó—Ö —Å—É–º—É
    • –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏—á —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é –∑ –∫–æ—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–∏–º–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–∏–º–∏

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 5. –¢–∏–ø –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó

    –Ø–≤–Ω–æ –∑–∞–¥–∞–π —Ç–∏–ø –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è, —è–∫–µ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è.

    • —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î string
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç–∏ —á–∏—Å–ª–æ
    • –ø—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ–∑—É–π –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫—É –∫–æ–º–ø—ñ–ª—è—Ü—ñ—ó

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 6. –¢–∏–ø void

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é, —è–∫–∞ –Ω—ñ—á–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î.

    • —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è –≤–∏–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –ø–æ–≤—ñ–¥–æ–º–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—è –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å
    • —Ç–∏–ø –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è ‚Äî void
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É—Ç–∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è —ñ –ø–æ–¥–∏–≤–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫—É

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 7. –¢–∏–ø never

    –ü—Ä–æ–¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–π –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∏–ø—É never.

    • —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é, —è–∫–∞ –∑–∞–≤–∂–¥–∏ –∫–∏–¥–∞—î –ø–æ–º–∏–ª–∫—É
    • –≤–∫–∞–∂–∏ —Ç–∏–ø –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è never
    • –ø–æ—è—Å–Ω–∏, —á–æ–º—É —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è –Ω—ñ—á–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—î

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 8. –¢–∏–ø—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—è –æ–± º—î–∫—Ç–∞

    –û–ø–∏—à–∏ —Ç–∏–ø –¥–ª—è –æ–± º—î–∫—Ç–∞ –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å–∏.

    • –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—ñ: street (string), house (number)
    • —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –æ–± º—î–∫—Ç –∑ —Ü–∏–º–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–∏–º–∏
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –∑–º—ñ–Ω–∏—Ç–∏ —Ç–∏–ø –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—ñ

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 9. –¢–∏–ø—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—è –º–∞—Å–∏–≤—É

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –º–∞—Å–∏–≤ –∑ —á–∏—Å–ª–∞–º–∏.

    • —Ç–∏–ø –º–∞—Å–∏–≤—É ‚Äî number[]
    • –¥–æ–¥–∞–π –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–∞ —á–∏—Å–µ–ª
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –¥–æ–¥–∞—Ç–∏ —Ä—è–¥–æ–∫

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 10. –î–≤–æ–≤–∏–º—ñ—Ä–Ω–∏–π –º–∞—Å–∏–≤

    –û–ø–∏—à–∏ –¥–≤–æ–≤–∏–º—ñ—Ä–Ω–∏–π –º–∞—Å–∏–≤ —á–∏—Å–µ–ª.

    • —Ç–∏–ø number[][]
    • –∑–∞–ø–æ–≤–Ω–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–∏–º–∏
    • –æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º–∞–π –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –¥–æ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∑ –µ–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 11. Tuple (–∫–æ—Ä—Ç–µ–∂)

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –∫–æ—Ä—Ç–µ–∂ –∑ —Ñ—ñ–∫—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–æ—é.

    • —Ç–∏–ø–∏: string, number, boolean
    • –∑–∞–ø–æ–≤–Ω–∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è–º–∏
    • —Å–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π –ø–æ—Ä—É—à–∏—Ç–∏ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 12. Enum

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ enum –¥–ª—è —Ä–æ–ª–µ–π –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞.

    • ADMIN, USER, GUEST
    • –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–π enum —É –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ–π
    • –≤–∏–≤–µ–¥–∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 13. Union —Ç–∏–ø–∏

    –í–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–π –æ–± º—î–¥–Ω–∞–Ω–Ω—è —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤.

    • –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ string –∞–±–æ number
    • –ø—Ä–∏—Å–≤–æ–π –æ–±–∏–¥–≤–∞ –≤–∞—Ä—ñ–∞–Ω—Ç–∏ –ø–æ —á–µ—Ä–∑—ñ
    • –ø—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª—ñ–∑—É–π –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∞–≥–∏

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 14. Type Narrowing

    –†–µ–∞–ª—ñ–∑—É–π —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—é –∑ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤—ñ—Ä–∫–æ—é —Ç–∏–ø—É.

    • –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç: string | number
    • —è–∫—â–æ string ‚Äî –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤–µ–¥–∏ —É –≤–µ—Ä—Ö–Ω—ñ–π —Ä–µ–≥—ñ—Å—Ç—Ä
    • —è–∫—â–æ number ‚Äî –æ–∫—Ä—É–≥–ª–∏

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 15. Type Alias

    –°—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ –ø—Å–µ–≤–¥–æ–Ω—ñ–º —Ç–∏–ø—É.

    • alias –¥–ª—è number | string
    • –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–π –π–æ–≥–æ —É —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó

// Task 4

  return num1 + num2;
}

  return str;
}

console.log(returnString("22"));
// console.log(returnString(22));
// Error: Argument of type 'number' is not assignable to parameter of type 'string'.

  console.log(str);
  // return str;
  // Error: Type 'string' is not assignable to type 'void'.
}

// Task 7

  throw new Error(message);
}

console.log(myObj);
// myObj.house = "32";
// Error: Type 'string' is not assignable to type 'number'.

// myArr.splice(0, 1, "55");
// Error: Argument of type 'string' is not assignable to parameter of type 'number'.

// –î–∞—î –¥–µ—è–∫—É –≥–Ω—É—á–∫—ñ—Å—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥—É –∞–ª–µ –Ω–µ –≤—Ç—Ä–∞—á–∞—î –∑–∞—Ö–∏—Å—Ç—É –≤—ñ–¥ "—à–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∏—Ö —Ä—É—á–æ–∫"

// Task 14

function getData(data: string | number) {
  if (typeof data === "string") {
    return data.toUpperCase();
  } else {
    return data.toFixed();
  }
}

console.log(getData("Twenty and one"));
console.log(getData(20.1));

// Task 15

type testAlias = number | string;

function getData2(data: testAlias) {
  if (typeof data === "string") {
    return data.toUpperCase();
  } else {
    return data.toFixed();
  }
}

console.log(getData2("Twenty and two"));
console.log(getData2(20.2));

    TypeScript: —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω—ñ —Ç–∏–ø–∏, —ñ–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–∏ —Ç–∞ –û–û–ü

    1. –©–æ —Ç–∞–∫–µ —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω—ñ —Ç–∏–ø–∏ (Complex Types)

    –°–∫–ª–∞–¥–Ω—ñ —Ç–∏–ø–∏ –≤ TypeScript ‚Äî —Ü–µ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω—ñ –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü—ñ—ó —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤, —è–∫—ñ –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—Ç—å —Ç–æ—á–Ω—ñ—à–µ –æ–ø–∏—Å—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—É –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö.

    –í–æ–Ω–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é—Ç—å—Å—è —Ä–∞–∑–æ–º –∑ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–∏–º–∏ —Ç–∏–ø–∞–º–∏ (string, number, boolean) —ñ —Ä–æ–±–ª—è—Ç—å –∫–æ–¥ –±—ñ–ª—å—à –Ω–∞–¥—ñ–π–Ω–∏–º —Ç–∞ —á–∏—Ç–∞–±–µ–ª—å–Ω–∏–º.

    2. Tuple (–∫–æ—Ä—Ç–µ–∂—ñ)

    Tuple ‚Äî —Ü–µ –º–∞—Å–∏–≤ —Ñ—ñ–∫—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ—ó –¥–æ–≤–∂–∏–Ω–∏, –¥–µ –∫–æ–∂–µ–Ω –µ–ª–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –º–∞—î —Å–≤—ñ–π —Ç–∏–ø. 

    let userData: [string, number, boolean] = ["Alex", 25, true];

    üëâ –ß–∞—Å—Ç–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–æ—Ö –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω—å –∑ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó.

    3. Enum

    Enum ‚Äî –Ω–∞–±—ñ—Ä —ñ–º–µ–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—Ö –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç–∞–Ω—Ç.

    enum Status {
  Active,
  Disabled,
  Pending

    üëâ –ó–∞ –∑–∞–º–æ–≤—á—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ—á–∏–Ω–∞—é—Ç—å—Å—è –∑ 0.

    4. Union —Ç–∏–ø–∏

    Union –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ–π –º–∞—Ç–∏ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –∑ –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–æ—Ö —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤. 

    let id: number | string;
id = 10;
id = "10";

    5. Intersection —Ç–∏–ø–∏

    Intersection –ø–æ—î–¥–Ω—É—î –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–∞ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤ –≤ –æ–¥–∏–Ω.

    8. Interface vs Type Alias

    • type ‚Äî —É–Ω—ñ–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ—à–∏–π (union, intersection)

    9. –ö–ª–∞—Å–∏ –≤ TypeScript

    10. –ú–æ–¥–∏—Ñ—ñ–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø—É

    14. Type Narrowing

// Task 1 & 2 & 3

interface Users {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  email?: string;
  readonly id: number;
}

const firstUser: Users = {
  name: "Bob",
  age: 12,
  id: 1,
};
const secondUser: Users = {
  name: "Bib",
  age: 52,
  email: "somemail@nomail.net",
  id: 2,
};

console.log(firstUser);
console.log(secondUser);
console.log(secondUser.id);
// secondUser.id = 12;
// console.log(secondUser.id);
// Error: Cannot assign to 'id' because it is a read-only property.

// Task 4

interface MathFunc {
  (x: number, y: number): number;
}

const addFunc: MathFunc = (x, y) => {
  return x + y;
};

const multiplyFunc: MathFunc = (x, y) => {
  return x * y;
};

console.log(addFunc(10, 25));
console.log(multiplyFunc(10, 25));

// Task 5

interface Person {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  email?: string;
  readonly id: number;
}

interface Employee extends Person {
  readonly salary: number;
}

const employeeBub: Employee = {
  name: "Bub",
  age: 22,
  email: "somemail2@nomail.net",
  id: 1,
  salary: 2500,
};

console.log(employeeBub);

// Task 8

interface Vehicle {
  brand: string;
  model: string;
  type: string;
  year: number;
  getInfo(): string;
}

class Car implements Vehicle {
  // brand: string;
  // model: string;
  // type: string;
  // year: number;

  // constructor(brand: string, model: string, type: string, year: number) {
  //   this.brand = brand;
  //   this.model = model;
  //   this.type = type;
  //   this.year = year;
  // }

  constructor(
    public brand: string,
    public model: string,
    public type: string,
    public year: number,
  ) {}

  getInfo(): string {
    return `Car: ${this.brand} ${this.model} Type: ${this.type} Year: ${this.year}`;
  }
}

const myBMW = new Car("BMW", "V55", "electro", 2026);

console.log(myBMW.getInfo());

// Task 9

class ChinaCar implements Vehicle {
  constructor(
    public brand: string,
    public model: string,
    public type: string,
    public year: number,
    private manufacture: string,
  ) {}

  getInfo(): string {
    return `Car: ${this.brand} ${this.model} Type: ${this.type} Year: ${this.year} Manufacturer: ${this.manufacture}`;
  }
}

const myFakeBMW = new ChinaCar("BMW", "V55", "electro", 2026, "China");

console.log(myFakeBMW.getInfo());
// console.log(myFakeBMW.manufacture);
// myFakeBMW.manufacture = "Germany";
// Error: Property 'manufacture' is private and only accessible within class 'ChinaCar'.

// Task 10

class BankAccount {
  private _balance: number = 0;

  constructor(initialBalance: number) {
    this.balance = initialBalance;
  }

  get balance(): number {
    return this._balance;
  }

  set balance(newValue: number) {
    if (newValue < 0) {
      return;
    }
    this._balance = newValue;
  }

  public deposit(amount: number): void {
    if (amount <= 0) {
      console.error("–°—É–º–∞ –¥–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç—É –º–∞—î –±—É—Ç–∏ –±—ñ–ª—å—à–æ—é –∑–∞ –Ω—É–ª—å");
      return;
    }
    this.balance += amount;
    console.log(`–ü–æ–ø–æ–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ ${amount}. –ü–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${this.balance}`);
  }

  public withdraw(amount: number): void {
    if (amount <= 0) {
      console.error("–°—É–º–∞ –∑–Ω—è—Ç—Ç—è –º–∞—î –±—É—Ç–∏ –±—ñ–ª—å—à–æ—é –∑–∞ –Ω—É–ª—å");
      return;
    }

    const previousBalance = this.balance;
    this.balance -= amount;

    if (this.balance === previousBalance) {
      console.error("–ó–Ω—è—Ç—Ç—è –≤—ñ–¥—Ö–∏–ª–µ–Ω–æ: –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–Ω—å–æ –∫–æ—à—Ç—ñ–≤.");
    } else {
      console.log(`–ó–Ω—è—Ç–æ ${amount}. –ó–∞–ª–∏—à–æ–∫: ${this.balance}`);
    }
  }
}

const myAccount = new BankAccount(100);

console.log(`–ú—ñ–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${myAccount.balance}`);

myAccount.balance = 500;
myAccount.balance = -200;
myAccount.deposit(200);
myAccount.withdraw(200);
myAccount.withdraw(2000);
console.log(`–ú—ñ–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${myAccount.balance}`);

    this.age = age;

      `This is ${this.firstName} ${this.lastName}, ${this.age}'s old`,
    );

interface Sound {
  makeSound(): void;
}

abstract class Animal implements Sound {
  constructor(public name: string) {}

  breathe() {
    console.log(`${this.name} –¥–∏—Ö–∞—î...`);
  }

  abstract makeSound(): void;
}

// const test = new Animal("–•—Ç–æ—Å—å");
// Error: Cannot create an instance of an abstract class.

class Dog extends Animal {
  makeSound() {
    console.log(`${this.name} –∫–∞–∂–µ: –ì–∞–≤-–≥–∞–≤!`);
  }
}

class Cat extends Animal {
  makeSound() {
    console.log(`${this.name} –∫–∞–∂–µ: –ú—è—É!`);
  }
}

const myDog = new Dog("–°—ñ—Ä–∫–æ");
myDog.breathe();
myDog.makeSound();

const myCat = new Cat("–ú—É—Ä–∫–æ");
myCat.breathe();
myCat.makeSound();

function interactWithAnimal(animal: Animal) {
  animal.breathe();
  animal.makeSound();

  if (animal instanceof Dog) {
    console.log(`${animal.name} –≤–∏–ª—è—î —Ö–≤–æ—Å—Ç–æ–º!`);
  }

  if (animal instanceof Cat) {
    console.log(`${animal.name} –º—É—Ä—á–∏—Ç—å...`);
  }
}

interactWithAnimal(myDog);
interactWithAnimal(myCat);

function getData(data: number | string) {
  if (typeof data === "string") {
    return data.split(" ").join(", ").toUpperCase();
  } else {
    return data * 2;
  }
}

console.log(getData("Twenty and two"));
console.log(getData(20.2));

interface IUser {
  id: number;
  userName: string;
  getRole(): string;
}

class BaseUser implements IUser {
  constructor(
    public readonly id: number,
    public userName: string,
    protected email: string,
  ) {}

  public getRole(): string {
    return "User";
  }

  public getContactInfo(): string {
    return `–ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á: ${this.userName}, Email: ${this.email}`;
  }
}

class NewAdmin extends BaseUser {
  private permissions: string[];

  constructor(
    id: number,
    userName: string,
    email: string,
    permissions: string[],
  ) {
    super(id, userName, email);
    this.permissions = permissions;
  }

  public override getRole(): string {
    return `Admin (–î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∏: ${this.permissions.join(", ")})`;
  }

  public checkSecurity(): void {
    console.log(`–ü–µ—Ä–µ–≤—ñ—Ä–∫–∞ –±–µ–∑–ø–µ–∫–∏ –¥–ª—è ${this.email}... –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª–µ–Ω–æ.`);
  }
}

const commonUser = new BaseUser(1, "ivan_petrov", "ivan@mail.com");
const superAdmin = new NewAdmin(99, "admin_boss", "boss@corp.com", [
  "delete_users",
  "edit_content",
]);

console.log(commonUser.getRole());
console.log(commonUser.getContactInfo());
console.log(superAdmin.getRole());
console.log(superAdmin.getContactInfo());

superAdmin.checkSecurity();
// commonUser.checkSecurity();
// Error: Property 'checkSecurity' does not exist on type 'BaseUser'.

// Task 10
class BankAccount {
  _balance = 0;
  constructor(initialBalance) {
    this.balance = initialBalance;
  }
  get balance() {
    return this._balance;
  }
  set balance(newValue) {
    if (newValue < 0) {
      return;
    }
    this._balance = newValue;
  }
  deposit(amount) {
    if (amount <= 0) {
      console.error("–°—É–º–∞ –¥–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç—É –º–∞—î –±—É—Ç–∏ –±—ñ–ª—å—à–æ—é –∑–∞ –Ω—É–ª—å");
      return;
    }
    this.balance += amount;
    console.log(`–ü–æ–ø–æ–≤–Ω–µ–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ ${amount}. –ü–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${this.balance}`);
  }
  withdraw(amount) {
    if (amount <= 0) {
      console.error("–°—É–º–∞ –∑–Ω—è—Ç—Ç—è –º–∞—î –±—É—Ç–∏ –±—ñ–ª—å—à–æ—é –∑–∞ –Ω—É–ª—å");
      return;
    }
    const previousBalance = this.balance;
    this.balance -= amount;
    if (this.balance === previousBalance) {
      console.error("–ó–Ω—è—Ç—Ç—è –≤—ñ–¥—Ö–∏–ª–µ–Ω–æ: –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–Ω—å–æ –∫–æ—à—Ç—ñ–≤.");
    } else {
      console.log(`–ó–Ω—è—Ç–æ ${amount}. –ó–∞–ª–∏—à–æ–∫: ${this.balance}`);
    }
  }
}
const myAccount = new BankAccount(100);
console.log(`–ú—ñ–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${myAccount.balance}`);
myAccount.balance = 500;
myAccount.balance = -200;
myAccount.deposit(200);
myAccount.withdraw(200);
myAccount.withdraw(2000);
console.log(`–ú—ñ–π –±–∞–ª–∞–Ω—Å: ${myAccount.balance}`);

    TypeScript: Generics, Function Overloading —Ç–∞ Decorators

    1. Function Overloading

    Function overloading –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—î –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç–∏ –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–∞ –≤–∞—Ä—ñ–∞–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ –≤–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫—É –æ–¥–Ω—ñ—î—ó —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó –∑ —Ä—ñ–∑–Ω–∏–º–∏ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞–º–∏.

    2. –ù–∞–≤—ñ—â–æ –ø–æ—Ç—Ä—ñ–±–µ–Ω Function Overloading

    –í—ñ–Ω –∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å–Ω–∏–π, –∫–æ–ª–∏ –æ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω–∞ –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –∑ —Ä—ñ–∑–Ω–∏–º–∏ –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä–∞–º–∏ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤, –∞–ª–µ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ç–∞—Ç–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–±–∞—á—É–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç.

    3. –Ø–∫ —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ overload-–∏

    
function makeDate(timestamp: number): Date;
function makeDate(m: number, d: number, y: number): Date;

function makeDate(mOrTimestamp: number, d?: number, y?: number): Date {
if (d !== undefined && y !== undefined) {
return new Date(y, mOrTimestamp, d);
} else {
return new Date(mOrTimestamp);
}
}

    4. Overload signatures vs implementation

    –°–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—ó –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º–∞ –∑–æ–≤–Ω—ñ ‚Äî TypeScript –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î —Ç—ñ–ª—å–∫–∏ overload-—Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä–∏.

    5. –°—É–º—ñ—Å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä

    Overload-—Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä–∏ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –±—É—Ç–∏ —Å—É–º—ñ—Å–Ω–∏–º–∏ –∑ —Ä–µ–∞–ª—ñ–∑–∞—Ü—ñ—î—é –∑–∞ —Ç–∏–ø–∞–º–∏ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç—ñ–≤ —ñ —Ç–∏–ø–æ–º –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—è.

    6. Generics: –Ω–∞–≤—ñ—â–æ –≤–æ–Ω–∏ –ø–æ—Ç—Ä—ñ–±–Ω—ñ

    Generics –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—Ç—å —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ —É–Ω—ñ–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó, –∫–ª–∞—Å–∏ —Ç–∞ —ñ–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–∏ –∑—ñ –∑–±–µ—Ä–µ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è–º —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤.

    7. Generics —É —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—è—Ö

    8. –†–æ–±–æ—Ç–∞ –∑ generic-–ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞–º–∏

    Generic-—Ç–∏–ø–∏ –Ω–µ –∑–Ω–∞—é—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö, –ø–æ–∫–∏ –º–∏ –Ω–µ –æ–±–º–µ–∂–∏–º–æ —ó—Ö.

    13. Generics —ñ –∫–ª–∞—Å–∏

    Generics –º–æ–∂—É—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∞—Ü—é–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –∑ –∫–ª–∞—Å–∞–º–∏ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —ó—Ö –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏.

    15. Decorators

    Decorators ‚Äî —Ü–µ —Å–ø–µ—Ü—ñ–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó, —è–∫—ñ –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—Ç—å –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ—ñ–∫—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –∫–ª–∞—Å–∏ —Ç–∞ —ó—Ö —á–ª–µ–Ω–∏.

    16. –î–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∏ –∫–ª–∞—Å—ñ–≤

    
function sealed(constructor: Function) {
  Object.seal(constructor);
  Object.seal(constructor.prototype);

    17. –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥ class decorator

  constructor(public title: string) {}

    18. Method decorators

    Method decorator –æ—Ç—Ä–∏–º—É—î target, —ñ–º'—è –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—É —Ç–∞ descriptor.

    19. Property decorators

    Property decorators –¥–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—Ç—å —Ä–µ–∞–≥—É–≤–∞—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –≤–ª–∞—Å—Ç–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç–µ–π –∫–ª–∞—Å—É.

    20. –ü—ñ–¥—Å—É–º–æ–∫

    • Function Overloading ‚Äî —Ä—ñ–∑–Ω—ñ —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä–∏ –æ–¥–Ω—ñ—î—ó —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó
    • Generics ‚Äî —É–Ω—ñ–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∞–ª—å–Ω—ñ—Å—Ç—å –±–µ–∑ –≤—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–∏ —Ç–∏–ø—ñ–≤
    • Decorators ‚Äî –º–µ—Ç–∞–ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º—É–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—è –≤ TypeScript
    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è

    –ü—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è: Generics, Function Overloading, Decorators

    –ó–∞–≤–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—è 2. Function Overloading –¥–ª—è —Ä–æ–±–æ—Ç–∏ –∑ –¥–∞–Ω–∏–º–∏

    • —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏ overload-—Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞—Ç—É—Ä–∏ –¥–ª—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü—ñ—ó formatData:

                  script.ts
//  Task 1

interface IEntity {
  id: number;
}

class Repository {
  private data: T[] = [];

  public add(item: T): void {
    this.data.push(item);
    console.log(`Add item with ID: ${item.id}`);
  }

  public getById(id: number): T | undefined {
    return this.data.find((item) => item.id === id);
  }

  public getAll(): T[] {
    return [...this.data];
  }
}

interface User extends IEntity {
  name: string;
  age: number;
  email: string;
}

const userRepository = new Repository();

userRepository.add({ id: 1, name: "Alex", age: 22, email: "alex@test.com" });
userRepository.add({ id: 2, name: "Maria", age: 25, email: "maria@test.com" });

const user = userRepository.getById(1);
console.log(user?.name);

// interface Product extends IEntity {
//   title: string;
//   price: number;
// }

//  Task 2

function formatData(value: string): string;
function formatData(value: number): string;
function formatData(value: Date): string;

function formatData(value: any): string {
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    return value.toUpperCase();
  } else if (typeof value === "number") {
    return `Number: ${value}`;
  } else if (value instanceof Date) {
    return value.toDateString();
  }
  return String(value);
}

console.log(formatData("12.02.2024"));
console.log(formatData(12022024));
console.log(formatData(new Date()));

//  Task 3

function LogMethod(
  target: any,
  propertyKey: string,
  descriptor: PropertyDescriptor,
) {
  const originalMethod = descriptor.value;

  descriptor.value = function (...args: any[]) {
    console.log(
      `[LOG]: –í–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—É "${propertyKey}" –∑ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏: ${JSON.stringify(args)}`,
    );

    const result = originalMethod.apply(this, args);

    return result;
  };

  return descriptor;
}

class UserService {
  @LogMethod
  createUser(name: string): void {
    console.log(`–ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞ ${name} —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–æ –≤ –±–∞–∑—ñ –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö.`);
  }

  @LogMethod
  deleteUser(id: number): void {
    console.log(`–ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞ –∑ ID ${id} –≤–∏–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–æ.`);
  }
}

const service = new UserService();
service.createUser("–û–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä");

service.deleteUser(42);

var __decorate =
  (this && this.__decorate) ||
  function (decorators, target, key, desc) {
    var c = arguments.length,
      r =
        c < 3
          ? target
          : desc === null
            ? (desc = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(target, key))
            : desc,
      d;
    if (typeof Reflect === "object" && typeof Reflect.decorate === "function")
      r = Reflect.decorate(decorators, target, key, desc);
    else
      for (var i = decorators.length - 1; i >= 0; i--)
        if ((d = decorators[i]))
          r = (c < 3 ? d(r) : c > 3 ? d(target, key, r) : d(target, key)) || r;
    return (c > 3 && r && Object.defineProperty(target, key, r), r);
  };

  }
  getAll() {
    return [...this.data];
  }
}

//  Task 3
function LogMethod(target, propertyKey, descriptor) {
  const originalMethod = descriptor.value;
  descriptor.value = function (...args) {
    console.log(
      `[LOG]: –í–∏–∫–ª–∏–∫ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—É "${propertyKey}" –∑ –∞—Ä–≥—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏: ${JSON.stringify(args)}`,
    );
    const result = originalMethod.apply(this, args);
    return result;
  };
  return descriptor;
}
class UserService {
  createUser(name) {
    console.log(`–ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞ ${name} —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–æ –≤ –±–∞–∑—ñ –¥–∞–Ω–∏—Ö.`);
  }
  deleteUser(id) {
    console.log(`–ö–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—É–≤–∞—á–∞ –∑ ID ${id} –≤–∏–¥–∞–ª–µ–Ω–æ.`);
  }
}
__decorate([LogMethod], UserService.prototype, "createUser", null);
__decorate([LogMethod], UserService.prototype, "deleteUser", null);
const service = new UserService();
service.createUser("–û–ª–µ–∫—Å–∞–Ω–¥—Ä");
service.deleteUser(42);
